[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m190[0m[39m:        for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mElement description : dataDescriptions[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m191[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m192[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mparseDescriptionRoot[0m[1;39m([0m[39mxmp, description[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m193[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m194[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m195[0m[39m:        return xmp;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m196[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m197[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m198[0m[39m:    private void [0m[1;35mparseDescriptionRoot[0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMPMetadata xmp, Element description[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrows XmpParsingException[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m199[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m200[0m[39m:        [0m[1;35mnsFinder.push[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdescription[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mxmpbox/src/main/java/org/apache/xmpbox/xml/DomXmpParser.jav[0m[1;92ma:79[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m85[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m:        try[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m:            DocumentBuilderFactory dbFactory = [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mDocumentBuilderFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mdbFactory.setNamespaceAware[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:            dBuilder = [0m[1;35mdbFactory.newDocumentBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m84[0m[39m:            nsFinder = new [0m[1;35mNamespaceFinder[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mxmpbox/src/main/java/org/apache/xmpbox/xml/DomXmpParser.jav[0m[1;92ma:79[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m85[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m:        try[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m81[0m[39m:            DocumentBuilderFactory dbFactory = [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mDocumentBuilderFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:            [0m[1;35mdbFactory.setNamespaceAware[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m83[0m[39m:            dBuilder = [0m[1;35mdbFactory.newDocumentBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m84[0m[39m:            nsFinder = new [0m[1;35mNamespaceFinder[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m85[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Identify root cause:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `DomXmpParser` constructor creates a `DocumentBuilderFactory` without [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdisabling external entity resolution or network-based DTD/schema loading. By [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefault, the Xerces parser will fetch external entities over HTTP/S, triggering the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSSRF sanitizer.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve existing logic:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must continue to build a namespace-aware DOM parser [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mdbFactory.setNamespaceAware[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All downstream parsing, comment removal, packet processing, and XMP metadata [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstruction must remain unchanged.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Tests and harness code must not be modified.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch plan:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. In `DomXmpParser.java` constructor [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m79[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m85[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, immediately after creating[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe `DocumentBuilderFactory` and before calling `[0m[1;35mnewDocumentBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, configure [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe factory to operate in “secure” mode:[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Enable JAXP secure processing:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         - `[0m[1;35mdbFactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMLConstants.FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING, true[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Disallow DOCTYPE declarations altogether:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         - [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mdbFactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http://apache.org/xml/features/disallow-doctype-decl"[0m[39m, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Disable resolution of external general and parameter entities:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         - [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mdbFactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http://xml.org/sax/features/external-general-entities"[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfalse[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         - [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mdbFactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http://xml.org/sax/features/external-parameter-entities"[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfalse[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Restrict access to external DTDs and schemas:[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         - `[0m[1;35mdbFactory.setAttribute[0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMLConstants.ACCESS_EXTERNAL_DTD, [0m[32m""[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         - `[0m[1;35mdbFactory.setAttribute[0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMLConstants.ACCESS_EXTERNAL_SCHEMA, [0m[32m""[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptional but recommended[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Install a no-op `EntityResolver` on the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`DocumentBuilder` to short-circuit any unexpected external-entity resolution:[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```java[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         dBuilder = [0m[1;35mdbFactory.newDocumentBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mdBuilder.setEntityResolver[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mpublicId, systemId[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m -> new [0m[1;35mInputSource[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStringReader[0m[1;39m([0m[32m""[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ```[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Wrap all feature/attribute calls in the existing [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ParserConfigurationException` catch block [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand catch `SAXNotRecognizedException` [0m[35m/[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`SAXNotSupportedException` if necessary[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, rethrowing an `XmpParsingException` with [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ErrorType.Configuration`.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Ensure imports are added for:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `javax.xml.XMLConstants`[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `org.xml.sax.EntityResolver`[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `org.xml.sax.InputSource`[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - `java.io.StringReader`[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand `org.xml.sax.SAXNotRecognizedException` [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.xml.sax.SAXNotSupportedException` if catching them explicitly[0m[1;39m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Disabling external entity resolution and DTD access is the industry-standard [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfix to prevent SSRF and XXE attacks in XML parsers.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer’s malicious XML can no longer trigger network fetches during [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mdBuilder.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, so `ServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrf` will not be invoked.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing parsing logic—comment stripping, processing instruction handling,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnode traversal—is untouched, so behavior for well-formed, safe XMP inputs remains [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe same.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Test coverage for XMP parsing will continue to pass, as valid XMP rarely [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrelies on external DTD/schema lookups.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential side effects & mitigation:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Very few [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif any[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m XMP payloads depend on external DTD/schema resolution; [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlegitimate inputs should parse normally.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If some downstream logic expects to load external schemas, it would now fail. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIn that edge case, introduce a custom `EntityResolver` that selectively allows [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mknown, whitelisted locals and still denies arbitrary URLs.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Logging or debugging can be added in the catch block for feature-setting [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfailures, to aid integration on different Java versions.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar hardening in other Apache libraries [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., disabling DOCTYPE in [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`XMLInputFactory`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m follows this pattern.[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - OWASP recommendations for JAXP secure processing.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mxmpbox/src/main/java/org/apache/xmpbox/xml/DomXmpParser.jav[0m[1;92ma:79[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m85[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mjava.xml/[0m[1;35mjavax.xml.parsers.DocumentBuilder.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mDocumentBuilder.jav[0m[1;92ma:122[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m[1;35morg.apache.xmpbox.xml.DomXmpParser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mDomXmpParser.jav[0m[1;92ma:113[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcom.example.DomXmpParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[39mDomXmpParserFuzzer.jav[0m[1;92ma:57[0m[1;39m)[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: 9e0307ad4945d0d0[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn SSRF [0m[1;39m([0m[39mServer-Side Request Forgery[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m issue was flagged by Jazzer when parsing XML [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min `DomXmpParser`. The fuzzer input triggered an HTTP connection to an external [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhost [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`jazze.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m via the default XML parser behavior. To mitigate, a patch was[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapplied to harden the XML parser by disabling external DTDs/entities, enabling [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecure processing, and installing a no-op `EntityResolver`. The patch also [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbroadened the exception handler to include `SAXNotRecognizedException` and [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`SAXNotSupportedException`. When building after this patch, the compiler reported [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat those two SAX exceptions “are never thrown in body of corresponding try [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstatement,” leading to a build failure in the XmpBox module.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Jazzer raised a `FuzzerSecurityIssueMedium: Server Side Request Forgery [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` when `DomXmpParser` fetched external XML content.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Stack trace shows the first network call occurs in the JDK’s `Socket.connect` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring an XML parse initiated by `javax.xml.parsers.DocumentBuilder.parse`.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The SSRF was triggered by untrusted input leading the parser to fetch a remote[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDTD or entity.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Key Observations  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The vulnerability arises from the default XML parser allowing external [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentities and DTD fetches.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`DomXmpParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m feeds arbitrary [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXML into `DomXmpParser.parse`, which uses the default JAXP configuration.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No explicit protections against external entities or network access were in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mplace.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `DomXmpParser.java`:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Imported `org.xml.sax.SAXNotRecognizedException`, [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.xml.sax.SAXNotSupportedException`, `org.xml.sax.EntityResolver`, [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.xml.sax.InputSource`, and `java.io.StringReader`.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • After obtaining `DocumentBuilderFactory dbFactory = [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mDocumentBuilderFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, added calls to:  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       – `[0m[1;35mdbFactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMLConstants.FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING, true[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       – [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mdbFactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http://apache.org/xml/features/disallow-doctype-decl"[0m[39m, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       – [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mdbFactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http://xml.org/sax/features/external-general-entities"[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfalse[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       – [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mdbFactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http://xml.org/sax/features/external-parameter-entities"[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfalse[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       – `[0m[1;35mdbFactory.setAttribute[0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMLConstants.ACCESS_EXTERNAL_DTD, [0m[32m""[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       – `[0m[1;35mdbFactory.setAttribute[0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMLConstants.ACCESS_EXTERNAL_SCHEMA, [0m[32m""[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Configured the `DocumentBuilder` with an `EntityResolver` that returns an [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mempty stream for any external entity:  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         new [0m[1;35mInputSource[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mStringReader[0m[1;39m([0m[32m""[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Broadened the existing `catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mParserConfigurationException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to `catch [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mParserConfigurationException | SAXNotRecognizedException | [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAXNotSupportedException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Build Outcome  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Maven compilation failed in XmpBox with errors indicating that [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`SAXNotRecognizedException` and `SAXNotSupportedException` “are never thrown in [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbody of corresponding try statement.”  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The erroneous catch clause prevents successful compilation; no other code [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanges were applied.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Review JAXP and `DocumentBuilderFactory#setFeature` signatures to determine [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich checked exceptions are actually thrown and need handling.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Inspect the existing `catch` scope and exception declarations in [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`DomXmpParser.java` to align with real thrown exceptions.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Audit other parsing entry points and factory configurations in the codebase to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensure consistent secure XML processing.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Examine differences in SAX feature support across JVM implementations to [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensure portability of the hardening code.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root Cause  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The build failure stems from catching `SAXNotRecognizedException` and [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`SAXNotSupportedException` in the same `try` block that calls methods [0m[1;39m([0m[39min this [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menvironment[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which only declare `ParserConfigurationException`. The compiler [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly flags that the SAX exceptions are never thrown by the enclosed calls, so [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe multi-catch is invalid.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We still need to harden the parser [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdisable external DTDs/entities, enable [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecure processing, install a no-op `EntityResolver`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to mitigate SSRF.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategy to Fix Compilation and Preserve SSRF Mitigation  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Split the configuration and builder‐creation into two distinct `try` blocks [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mso that each only catches exactly the checked exceptions its body can throw.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. In the first `try`, invoke all `[0m[1;35msetFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` calls [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich per JAXP spec [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcan throw `ParserConfigurationException`, `SAXNotRecognizedException`, [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`SAXNotSupportedException`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, plus the attribute calls [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich throw unchecked[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCatch those three exceptions together and wrap them in `XmpParsingException`.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. In a second `try`, call `[0m[1;35mnewDocumentBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich only throws [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ParserConfigurationException`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and catch just that one exception.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. After obtaining the `DocumentBuilder`, register a no-op `EntityResolver` and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitialize `NamespaceFinder`.  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Steps to Implement  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `DomXmpParser.java`, locate the constructor or initialization block around [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe existing `try`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mParserConfigurationException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rewrite it as follows [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpseudocode outline—adjust indent and exact variable [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnames to match the file[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     DocumentBuilderFactory dbFactory = [0m[1;35mDocumentBuilderFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mdbFactory.setNamespaceAware[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Secure‐processing feature configuration[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mdbFactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMLConstants.FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING, true[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mdbFactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http://apache.org/xml/features/disallow-doctype-decl[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"[0m[39m, true[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mdbFactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http://xml.org/sax/features/external-general-entitie[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32ms"[0m[39m, false[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mdbFactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http://xml.org/sax/features/external-parameter-entit[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mies"[0m[39m, false[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mdbFactory.setAttribute[0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMLConstants.ACCESS_EXTERNAL_DTD, [0m[32m""[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mdbFactory.setAttribute[0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMLConstants.ACCESS_EXTERNAL_SCHEMA, [0m[32m""[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mParserConfigurationException | SAXNotRecognizedException | [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAXNotSupportedException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         throw new [0m[1;35mXmpParsingException[0m[1;39m([0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             ErrorType.Configuration,[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[32m"Failed to configure XML parser for secure processing"[0m[39m,[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             e[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Builder creation[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         dBuilder = [0m[1;35mdbFactory.newDocumentBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mParserConfigurationException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         throw new [0m[1;35mXmpParsingException[0m[1;39m([0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             ErrorType.Configuration,[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[32m"Failed to initialize DocumentBuilder"[0m[39m,[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             e[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Disable any external entity resolution at parse time[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mdBuilder.setEntityResolver[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mpublicId, systemId[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ->[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         new [0m[1;35mInputSource[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mStringReader[0m[1;39m([0m[32m""[0m[39m, [0m[35m/[0m[39m* empty content *[0m[35m/[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Namespace handling[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     nsFinder = new [0m[1;35mNamespaceFinder[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove the old single `try [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mParserConfigurationException | [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAXNotRecognizedException | SAXNotSupportedException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` entirely.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure the imports include:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     import org.xml.sax.SAXNotRecognizedException;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     import org.xml.sax.SAXNotSupportedException;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     import org.xml.sax.EntityResolver;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     import org.xml.sax.InputSource;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     import java.io.StringReader;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Leave the parsing method’s existing `catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSAXException | IOException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification and Preservation of Functionality  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Splitting the `try` blocks aligns each catch with the exact exceptions [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeclared by the enclosed calls, resolving the “never thrown” compilation errors.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All secure features [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING`, DTD/entity disabling, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ACCESS_EXTERNAL_*`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remain set, and the no-op `EntityResolver` ensures any attempt[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto load an external entity returns an empty stream. This fully mitigates the SSRF [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreported by Jazzer.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing parsing logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mdBuilder.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and exception handling [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`catch [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSAXException | IOException`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are untouched, so existing tests and downstream [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconsumers of `DomXmpParser` will operate as before, apart from being protected [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39magainst external-entity loading.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Strictly forbidding DTD declarations and external entities can cause some [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalid XML inputs that rely on internal DTD subsets or external schema references to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfail. If that scenario arises, consider:  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Providing a whitelist of safe system IDs and resolving them locally, or  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • Customizing the `EntityResolver` to allow known safe entities.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other parts of the codebase are changed, so no broader impact is expected. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Testing & Verification  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rebuild the `xmpbox` module under the targeted JVM to verify compilation [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpasses.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Re-run the existing unit/integration tests to ensure no regressions.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Re-execute the Jazzer harness: confirm that attempts to load external entities[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor DTDs are blocked and that no SSRF is triggered.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Optionally test under multiple JVM implementations [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOracle JDK, OpenJ9, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto ensure feature configuration calls behave consistently.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcom.example.DomXmpParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[39mDomXmpParserFuzzer.jav[0m[1;92ma:57[0m[1;39m)[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: 9e0307ad4945d0d0[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn SSRF security issue was detected in the Apache XmpBox DOM parser when the fuzzer[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggered an HTTP connection [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`java.net.Socket.connect`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m during XML parsing. A [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch was proposed to harden the XML parser by enabling secure processing, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdisabling external DTDs and general/parameter entities, restricting external [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mschema/DTD access, and installing a no-op `EntityResolver`. After applying these [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanges, the build fails with two compilation errors in `DomXmpParser.java`, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstating that `org.xml.sax.SAXNotRecognizedException` and [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.xml.sax.SAXNotSupportedException` are “never thrown in body of corresponding [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtry statement.”[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial Issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A Jazzer fuzzing harness for `DomXmpParser` triggered a [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueMedium: Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` when parsing [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalicious XML.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The stack trace shows the call chain from `DomXmpParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m→ `DomXmpParser.parse` → `DocumentBuilder.parse` → underlying `HttpURLConnection` →[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Socket.connect`.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The issue indicates that untrusted XML input can cause outbound connections, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpotentially exposing internal services or allowing data exfiltration.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImportant Observations  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The vulnerability manifests when the XML parser attempts to resolve external [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentities or fetch resources over HTTP.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The error originates in Java’s XML parsing machinery [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`XML11Configuration.parse`,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`XMLParser.parse`, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m rather than in custom application logic.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The SSRF detector [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrf`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m flags the connection to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`jazze.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m` as a security violation.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- In `DomXmpParser.java` constructor:  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Instantiate `DocumentBuilderFactory` early and set `[0m[33mnamespaceAware[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m[39m`.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. In a `try` block, enable `XMLConstants.FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING`, disable [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDOCTYPE declarations, external general/parameter entities, and clear [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ACCESS_EXTERNAL_DTD`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`ACCESS_EXTERNAL_SCHEMA`.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Catch `ParserConfigurationException`, `SAXNotRecognizedException`, and [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`SAXNotSupportedException` to wrap them in `XmpParsingException`.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Create the `DocumentBuilder`, catching `ParserConfigurationException` for [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitialization errors.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Attach an `EntityResolver` that returns an empty `InputSource`.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Initialize `nsFinder`.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Result  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The Maven build fails with two compilation errors in `DomXmpParser.java` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m97[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    • “exception org.xml.sax.SAXNotRecognizedException is never thrown in body of [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorresponding try statement”  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    • “exception org.xml.sax.SAXNotSupportedException is never thrown in body of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorresponding try statement”  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- These errors indicate that the code within the `try` block only throws [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ParserConfigurationException`, so the additional SAX exceptions are invalid catch [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtargets.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAreas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Review which exceptions `DocumentBuilderFactory.setFeature` and `setAttribute` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mactually declare. Remove or adjust the `catch` clauses to match thrown exceptions. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Audit all XML-related parsing modules [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., any other XMP or PDF metadata [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsers[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for consistent secure configuration.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Examine the construction and use of `DocumentBuilderFactory` across the codebase [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto ensure uniform handling of external entities and external references.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Verify that the `EntityResolver` override correctly prevents network access in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mall parsing scenarios and does not break legitimate parsing of embedded data.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Check build tooling and Java version compatibility for SAX feature support and [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception declarations.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
