[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[39m*****************************************************************************[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m: * [0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m: * Licensed to the Apache Software Foundation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mASF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m under one[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m: * or more contributor license agreements.  See the NOTICE file[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m: * distributed with this work for additional information[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m: * regarding copyright ownership.  The ASF licenses this file[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m: * to you under the Apache License, Version [0m[1;36m2.0[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m: * [0m[32m"License"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; you may not use this file except in compliance[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Consolidate XML parser configuration and builder initialization into a single [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtry‐catch that only catches ParserConfigurationException:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Start by instantiating the DocumentBuilderFactory and enabling namespace [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mawareness.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Inside a single `try` block, call:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `[0m[1;35mdbFactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMLConstants.FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING, true[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mdbFactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http://apache.org/xml/features/disallow-doctype-decl"[0m[39m, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mdbFactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http://xml.org/sax/features/external-general-entities"[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfalse[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mdbFactory.setFeature[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"http://xml.org/sax/features/external-parameter-entities"[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfalse[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `[0m[1;35mdbFactory.setAttribute[0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMLConstants.ACCESS_EXTERNAL_DTD, [0m[32m""[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `[0m[1;35mdbFactory.setAttribute[0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMLConstants.ACCESS_EXTERNAL_SCHEMA, [0m[32m""[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `dBuilder = [0m[1;35mdbFactory.newDocumentBuilder[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `nsFinder = new [0m[1;35mNamespaceFinder[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Catch only `ParserConfigurationException` and wrap it in `XmpParsingException`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith an appropriate error message.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Remove invalid catch clauses for `SAXNotRecognizedException` and [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`SAXNotSupportedException`:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - These exceptions are not declared by any of the `setFeature` or `setAttribute`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalls on `DocumentBuilderFactory`, so they must be eliminated to fix the [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompilation errors.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. After the try‐catch, install the no‐op `EntityResolver` on the [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`DocumentBuilder`:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Use `[0m[1;35mdBuilder.setEntityResolver[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m[1;35mEntityResolver[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m public InputSource [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mresolveEntity[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString publicId, String systemId[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m return new [0m[1;35mInputSource[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStringReader[0m[1;39m([0m[32m""[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m [0m[1;39m}[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This ensures that any external entity resolution is redirected to an empty [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msource, fully blocking outbound SSRF attempts.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Update imports:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove imports for `org.xml.sax.SAXNotRecognizedException` and [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.xml.sax.SAXNotSupportedException`.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add imports for:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `org.xml.sax.EntityResolver`[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `org.xml.sax.InputSource`[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `java.io.StringReader`[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Retain existing imports for `javax.xml.XMLConstants`, `javax.xml.parsers.*`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand other DOM/SAX classes.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Verify no other code or tests reference the removed SAX exception types, to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensure clean compilation.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRationale:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- By catching only `ParserConfigurationException`, we align the catch targets with [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe actual exception declarations of `setFeature`, `setAttribute`, and [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`newDocumentBuilder`. This resolves the compilation errors.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All hardening configurations [0m[1;39m([0m[39msecure processing, disallow DTDs, block external [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentities and schemas[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the no‐op `EntityResolver` remain intact, fully [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maddressing the SSRF vulnerability.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The unified try‐catch preserves existing initialization logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnamespace [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mawareness, namespace finder[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and does not alter the parsing API or harness code.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Removing extraneous catches has no side effects on runtime behavior.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This pattern matches similar secure‐processing setups elsewhere in the codebase, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensuring consistency.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
